ListStreams

https://docs.aws.amazon.com/amazondynamodb/latest/APIReference/API_streams_ListStreams.html

    49	    public StreamDescription enableStream(String tableName, String tableArn, String viewType, String region) {
    50	        String key = streamKey(region, tableName);
    51	        StreamDescription existing = streams.get(key);
    52	        if (existing != null && "ENABLED".equals(existing.getStreamStatus())) {
    53	            return existing;
    54	        }
    55	
    56	        Instant now = Instant.now();
    57	        String label = STREAM_LABEL_FORMAT.format(now);
    58	        String streamArn = tableArn + "/stream/" + label;
    59	
    60	        StreamDescription sd = new StreamDescription();
    61	        sd.setStreamArn(streamArn);
    62	        sd.setStreamLabel(label);
    63	        sd.setStreamStatus("ENABLED");

    66	        sd.setCreationDateTime(now);

    72	        return sd;

   103	        String sequenceNumber = String.format("%021d", seq);
   104	
   105	        JsonNode sourceItem = newItem != null ? newItem : oldItem;
   106	        ObjectNode keys = buildKeys(sourceItem, table);
   107	
   108	        String viewType = sd.getStreamViewType();
   109	        JsonNode newImage = buildImage(newItem, viewType, true);
   110	        JsonNode oldImage = buildImage(oldItem, viewType, false);
   111	
   112	        DynamoDbStreamRecord record = new DynamoDbStreamRecord();
   113	        record.setEventId(UUID.randomUUID().toString());
   114	        record.setEventVersion("1.1");
   115	        record.setEventName(eventName);
   116	        record.setEventSource("aws:dynamodb");
   117	        record.setAwsRegion(region);
   118	        record.setSequenceNumber(sequenceNumber);
   119	        record.setApproximateCreationDateTime(Instant.now().getEpochSecond());
   120	        record.setKeys(keys);
   121	        record.setNewImage(newImage);
   122	        record.setOldImage(oldImage);
   123	        record.setStreamViewType(viewType);
   124	
   125	        ConcurrentLinkedDeque<DynamoDbStreamRecord> deque = records.get(sd.getStreamArn());
   126	        if (deque != null) {
   127	            deque.addLast(record);
   128	            while (deque.size() > MAX_RECORDS) {
   129	                deque.pollFirst();
   130	            }
   131	        }
   132	    }
   133	
   134	    private ObjectNode buildKeys(JsonNode item, TableDefinition table) {
   135	        ObjectNode keys = objectMapper.createObjectNode();
   136	        if (item == null) {
   137	            return keys;
   138	        }
   139	        for (KeySchemaElement ks : table.getKeySchema()) {
   140	            String attrName = ks.getAttributeName();
   141	            if (item.has(attrName)) {
   142	                keys.set(attrName, item.get(attrName));
   143	            }
   144	        }
   145	        return keys;
   146	    }
   147	
   148	    private JsonNode buildImage(JsonNode item, String viewType, boolean isNewImage) {
   149	        if (item == null) {
   150	            return null;
   151	        }
   152	        return switch (viewType) {
   153	            case "KEYS_ONLY" -> null;
   154	            case "NEW_IMAGE" -> isNewImage ? item : null;
   155	            case "OLD_IMAGE" -> !isNewImage ? item : null;
   156	            case "NEW_AND_OLD_IMAGES" -> item;
   157	            default -> null;
   158	        };
   159	    }
   160	
   161	    public List<StreamDescription> listStreams(String tableNameFilter, String region) {
   162	        List<StreamDescription> result = new ArrayList<>();
   163	        for (StreamDescription sd : streams.values()) {
   164	            if (tableNameFilter != null && !tableNameFilter.equals(sd.getTableName())) {
   165	                continue;
   166	            }
   167	            if (region != null && !sd.getStreamArn().contains(":" + region + ":")) {
   168	                continue;
   169	            }
   170	            result.add(sd);
   171	        }
   172	        return result;
   173	    }
   174	
   175	    public StreamDescription describeStream(String streamArn) {
   176	        for (StreamDescription sd : streams.values()) {
   177	            if (streamArn.equals(sd.getStreamArn())) {
   178	                return sd;
   179	            }
   180	        }
   181	        throw new AwsException("ResourceNotFoundException",
   182	                "Stream not found: " + streamArn, 400);
   183	    }
   184	
   185	    public String getShardIterator(String streamArn, String shardId,
   186	                                   String iteratorType, String sequenceNumber) {
   187	        StreamDescription sd = describeStream(streamArn);
   188	        if (!"ENABLED".equals(sd.getStreamStatus()) && !"DISABLED".equals(sd.getStreamStatus())) {
   189	            throw new AwsException("ResourceNotFoundException",
   190	                    "Stream not found: " + streamArn, 400);
   191	        }
   192	
   193	        ConcurrentLinkedDeque<DynamoDbStreamRecord> deque = records.get(streamArn);
   194	        List<DynamoDbStreamRecord> snapshot = deque != null ? new ArrayList<>(deque) : List.of();
   195	
   196	        int position = switch (iteratorType) {
   197	            case "TRIM_HORIZON" -> 0;
   198	            case "LATEST" -> snapshot.size();
   199	            case "AT_SEQUENCE_NUMBER" -> findSequencePosition(snapshot, sequenceNumber, false);
   200	            case "AFTER_SEQUENCE_NUMBER" -> findSequencePosition(snapshot, sequenceNumber, true);
   201	            default -> throw new AwsException("ValidationException",
   202	                    "Unknown iterator type: " + iteratorType, 400);
   203	        };
   204	
   205	        return encodeIterator(streamArn, position);
   206	    }
   207	
   208	    private int findSequencePosition(List<DynamoDbStreamRecord> records, String targetSeq, boolean after) {
   209	        for (int i = 0; i < records.size(); i++) {
   210	            String seq = records.get(i).getSequenceNumber();
   211	            int cmp = seq.compareTo(targetSeq);
   212	            if (after ? cmp > 0 : cmp >= 0) {
   213	                return i;
   214	            }
   215	        }
   216	        return records.size();
   217	    }
   218	
   219	    public record GetRecordsResult(List<DynamoDbStreamRecord> records, String nextShardIterator) {}
   220	
   221	    public GetRecordsResult getRecords(String shardIterator, Integer limit) {
   222	        String[] parts = decodeIterator(shardIterator);
   223	        String streamArn = parts[0];
   224	        int position = Integer.parseInt(parts[1]);
   225	
   226	        ConcurrentLinkedDeque<DynamoDbStreamRecord> deque = records.get(streamArn);
   227	        List<DynamoDbStreamRecord> snapshot = deque != null ? new ArrayList<>(deque) : List.of();
   228	
   229	        int effectiveLimit = limit != null ? limit : 100;
   230	        int end = Math.min(position + effectiveLimit, snapshot.size());
   231	        List<DynamoDbStreamRecord> page = snapshot.subList(position, end);
   232	
   233	        String nextIterator = encodeIterator(streamArn, end);
   234	        return new GetRecordsResult(new ArrayList<>(page), nextIterator);
   235	    }
   236	
   237	    private String encodeIterator(String streamArn, int position) {
   238	        String raw = streamArn + "|" + position;
   239	        return Base64.getEncoder().encodeToString(raw.getBytes());
   240	    }
   241	
   242	    private String[] decodeIterator(String iterator) {
   243	        try {
   244	            String raw = new String(Base64.getDecoder().decode(iterator));
   245	            int lastPipe = raw.lastIndexOf('|');
   246	            if (lastPipe < 0) {
   247	                throw new AwsException("ValidationException", "Invalid shard iterator", 400);
   248	            }
   249	            return new String[]{raw.substring(0, lastPipe), raw.substring(lastPipe + 1)};
   250	        } catch (IllegalArgumentException e) {
   251	            throw new AwsException("ValidationException", "Invalid shard iterator", 400);
   252	        }
   253	    }
   254	
   255	    private String streamKey(String region, String tableName) {
   256	        return region + "::" + tableName;
   257	    }
   258	}

   121	    public TableDefinition createTable(String tableName,
   122	                                        List<KeySchemaElement> keySchema,

   125	                                        List<GlobalSecondaryIndex> gsis,

   319	    public UpdateResult updateItem(String tableName, JsonNode key, JsonNode attributeUpdates,
   320	                                    String updateExpression,
   321	                                    JsonNode expressionAttrNames, JsonNode expressionAttrValues,
   322	                                    String returnValues, String conditionExpression, String region) {
   323	        String storageKey = regionKey(region, tableName);
   324	        TableDefinition table = tableStore.get(storageKey)
   325	                .orElseThrow(() -> resourceNotFoundException(tableName));
   326	
   327	        String itemKey = buildItemKey(table, key);
   328	        var items = itemsByTable.computeIfAbsent(storageKey, k -> new ConcurrentSkipListMap<>());
   329	
   330	        // Get existing item or create new one from key
   331	        JsonNode existing = items.get(itemKey);
   332	
   333	        if (conditionExpression != null) {
   334	            evaluateCondition(existing, conditionExpression, expressionAttrNames, expressionAttrValues);
   335	        }
   336	
   337	        ObjectNode item;
   338	        if (existing != null) {
   339	            item = existing.deepCopy();
   340	        } else {
   341	            item = key.deepCopy();
   342	        }
   343	
   344	        // Apply UpdateExpression (modern format: "SET #n = :val, age = :age REMOVE attr")
   345	        if (updateExpression != null) {
   346	            applyUpdateExpression(item, updateExpression, expressionAttrNames, expressionAttrValues);
   347	        }
   348	        // Apply attribute updates (legacy format: AttributeUpdates)
   349	        else if (attributeUpdates != null && attributeUpdates.isObject()) {
   350	            Iterator<Map.Entry<String, JsonNode>> fields = attributeUpdates.fields();
   351	            while (fields.hasNext()) {
   352	                var entry = fields.next();
   353	                String attrName = entry.getKey();
   354	                JsonNode update = entry.getValue();

   356	                JsonNode value = update.get("Value");
   357	
   358	                switch (action) {
   359	                    case "PUT" -> { if (value != null) item.set(attrName, value); }
   360	                    case "DELETE" -> item.remove(attrName);
   361	                    case "ADD" -> {
   362	                        // Simple ADD for numeric values
   363	                        if (value != null) item.set(attrName, value);
   364	                    }
   365	                }
   366	            }
   367	        }
   368	
   369	        items.put(itemKey, item);
   370	        persistItems(storageKey);
   371	
   372	        if (streamService != null) {
   373	            streamService.captureEvent(tableName, "MODIFY", existing, item, table, region);
   374	        }
   375	
   376	        return new UpdateResult(item, existing);
   377	    }

   386	    public QueryResult query(String tableName, JsonNode keyConditions,
   387	                              JsonNode expressionAttrValues, String keyConditionExpression,
   388	                              String filterExpression, Integer limit, String region) {
   389	        return query(tableName, keyConditions, expressionAttrValues, keyConditionExpression,
   390	                     filterExpression, limit, null, null, null, null, region);

   393	    public QueryResult query(String tableName, JsonNode keyConditions,
   394	                              JsonNode expressionAttrValues, String keyConditionExpression,
   395	                              String filterExpression, Integer limit, Boolean scanIndexForward, String indexName,
   396	                              JsonNode exclusiveStartKey, JsonNode exprAttrNames, String region) {
   397	        String storageKey = regionKey(region, tableName);
   398	        TableDefinition table = tableStore.get(storageKey)
   399	                .orElseThrow(() -> resourceNotFoundException(tableName));
   400	
   401	        var items = itemsByTable.get(storageKey);
   402	        if (items == null) return new QueryResult(List.of(), 0, null);
   403	
   404	        // Resolve key names: use GSI or table keys
   405	        String pkName;
   406	        String skName;
   407	        if (indexName != null) {
   408	            var gsi = table.findGsi(indexName);
   409	            if (gsi.isPresent()) {
   410	                pkName = gsi.get().getPartitionKeyName();
   411	                skName = gsi.get().getSortKeyName();
   412	            } else {
   413	                var lsi = table.findLsi(indexName)
   414	                        .orElseThrow(() -> new AwsException("ValidationException",
   415	                                "The table does not have the specified index: " + indexName, 400));
   416	                pkName = lsi.getPartitionKeyName();
   417	                skName = lsi.getSortKeyName();
   418	            }
   419	        } else {
   420	            pkName = table.getPartitionKeyName();
   421	            skName = table.getSortKeyName();
   422	        }
   423	
   424	        List<JsonNode> results = new ArrayList<>();
   425	
   426	        if (keyConditions != null) {
   427	            // Legacy KeyConditions format
   428	            JsonNode pkCondition = keyConditions.get(pkName);
   429	            String pkValue = extractComparisonValue(pkCondition);
   430	
   431	            for (JsonNode item : items.values()) {
   432	                if (!item.has(pkName)) continue;
   433	                if (matchesAttributeValue(item.get(pkName), pkValue)) {
   434	                    if (skName != null && keyConditions.has(skName)) {
   435	                        JsonNode skCondition = keyConditions.get(skName);
   436	                        if (matchesKeyCondition(item.get(skName), skCondition)) {
   437	                            results.add(item);
   438	                        }
   439	                    } else {
   440	                        results.add(item);
   441	                    }
   442	                }
   443	            }
   444	        } else if (keyConditionExpression != null) {
   445	            // Modern expression format with exprAttrNames support
   446	            results = queryWithExpression(items, pkName, skName, keyConditionExpression,
   447	                                          expressionAttrValues, exprAttrNames);
   448	        }
   449	
   450	        // Filter out items without GSI key if querying GSI (sparse index)
   451	        if (indexName != null) {
   452	            String finalPkName = pkName;
   453	            results = results.stream().filter(item -> item.has(finalPkName)).toList();
   454	        }
   455	
   456	        // Filter out TTL-expired items
   457	        results = results.stream().filter(item -> !isExpired(item, table)).toList();
   458	
   459	        // Sort by sort key if present
   460	        if (skName != null) {
   461	            String finalSkName = skName;
   462	            results = new ArrayList<>(results);
   463	            results.sort((a, b) -> {
   464	                String aVal = extractScalarValue(a.get(finalSkName));
   465	                String bVal = extractScalarValue(b.get(finalSkName));
   466	                if (aVal == null && bVal == null) return 0;
   467	                if (aVal == null) return -1;
   468	                if (bVal == null) return 1;
   469	                return compareValues(aVal, bVal);
   470	            });
   471	            if (Boolean.FALSE.equals(scanIndexForward)) {
   472	                Collections.reverse(results);
   473	            }
   474	        }
   475	
   476	        // Apply ExclusiveStartKey offset
   477	        if (exclusiveStartKey != null) {
   478	            TableDefinition finalTable = table;
   479	            String startItemKey = buildItemKeyFromNode(exclusiveStartKey, pkName, skName);
   480	            int startIdx = -1;
   481	            for (int i = 0; i < results.size(); i++) {
   482	                String thisKey = buildItemKeyFromNode(results.get(i), pkName, skName);
   483	                if (thisKey.equals(startItemKey)) {
   484	                    startIdx = i;
   485	                    break;
   486	                }
   487	            }
   488	            if (startIdx >= 0) {
   489	                results = new ArrayList<>(results.subList(startIdx + 1, results.size()));
   490	            }
   491	        }
   492	
   493	        List<JsonNode> evaluatedItems = results;
   494	        JsonNode lastEvaluatedKey = null;
   495	
   496	        if (limit != null && limit > 0 && evaluatedItems.size() > limit) {
   497	            JsonNode lastItem = evaluatedItems.get(limit - 1);
   498	            lastEvaluatedKey = buildKeyNode(table, lastItem, pkName, skName);
   499	            evaluatedItems = new ArrayList<>(evaluatedItems.subList(0, limit));
   500	        }
   501	
   502	        int scannedCount = evaluatedItems.size();
   503	
   504	        if (filterExpression != null) {
   505	            evaluatedItems = evaluatedItems.stream()
   506	                    .filter(item -> matchesFilterExpression(item, filterExpression,
   507	                            exprAttrNames, expressionAttrValues))
   508	                    .toList();
   509	        }
   510	
   511	        return new QueryResult(evaluatedItems, scannedCount, lastEvaluatedKey);
   512	    }

   514	    public ScanResult scan(String tableName, String filterExpression,
   515	                            JsonNode expressionAttrNames, JsonNode expressionAttrValues,
   516	                            JsonNode scanFilter, Integer limit, JsonNode exclusiveStartKey) {
   517	        return scan(tableName, filterExpression, expressionAttrNames, expressionAttrValues,
   518	                    scanFilter, limit, exclusiveStartKey, regionResolver.getDefaultRegion());
   519	    }
   520	
   521	    public ScanResult scan(String tableName, String filterExpression,
   522	                            JsonNode expressionAttrNames, JsonNode expressionAttrValues,
   523	                            JsonNode scanFilter, Integer limit, JsonNode exclusiveStartKey, String region) {
   524	        String storageKey = regionKey(region, tableName);
   525	        TableDefinition table = tableStore.get(storageKey)
   526	                .orElseThrow(() -> resourceNotFoundException(tableName));
   527	
   528	        var items = itemsByTable.get(storageKey);
   529	        if (items == null) return new ScanResult(List.of(), 0, null);
   530	
   531	        // ConcurrentSkipListMap keeps items sorted by item key — no sort needed.
   532	        // Use tailMap for O(log n) pagination instead of O(n) linear search.
   533	        String pkName = table.getPartitionKeyName();
   534	        String skName = table.getSortKeyName();
   535	
   536	        var source = exclusiveStartKey != null
   537	                ? items.tailMap(buildItemKeyFromNode(exclusiveStartKey, pkName, skName), false).values()
   538	                : items.values();
   539	
   540	        int totalScanned = 0;
   541	        List<JsonNode> results = new ArrayList<>();
   542	        for (JsonNode item : source) {
   543	            totalScanned++;
   544	            if (isExpired(item, table)) {
   545	                continue;
   546	            }
   547	            if (filterExpression != null
   548	                    && !matchesFilterExpression(item, filterExpression, expressionAttrNames, expressionAttrValues)) {
   549	                continue;
   550	            }
   551	            if (scanFilter != null && !matchesScanFilter(item, scanFilter)) {
   552	                continue;
   553	            }
   554	            results.add(item);
   555	        }
   556	
   557	        JsonNode lastEvaluatedKey = null;
   558	        if (limit != null && limit > 0 && results.size() > limit) {
   559	            JsonNode lastItem = results.get(limit - 1);
   560	            lastEvaluatedKey = buildKeyNode(table, lastItem, pkName, skName);
   561	            results = results.subList(0, limit);
   562	        }
   563	
   564	        return new ScanResult(results, totalScanned, lastEvaluatedKey);
   565	    }
   566	
   567	    private boolean matchesScanFilter(JsonNode item, JsonNode scanFilter) {
   568	        Iterator<Map.Entry<String, JsonNode>> fields = scanFilter.fields();
   569	        while (fields.hasNext()) {
   570	            var entry = fields.next();
   571	            String attrName = entry.getKey();
   572	            JsonNode condition = entry.getValue();
   573	            JsonNode attrValue = item.get(attrName);
   574	            if (!matchesKeyCondition(attrValue, condition)) {
   575	                return false;
   576	            }
   577	        }
   578	        return true;
   579	    }

   581	    // --- Batch Operations ---
   582	
   583	    public record BatchWriteResult(Map<String, List<JsonNode>> unprocessedItems) {}
   584	
   585	    public BatchWriteResult batchWriteItem(Map<String, List<JsonNode>> requestItems, String region) {
   586	        for (Map.Entry<String, List<JsonNode>> entry : requestItems.entrySet()) {
   587	            String tableName = entry.getKey();
   588	            for (JsonNode writeRequest : entry.getValue()) {
   589	                if (writeRequest.has("PutRequest")) {
   590	                    JsonNode item = writeRequest.get("PutRequest").get("Item");
   591	                    putItem(tableName, item, region);
   592	                } else if (writeRequest.has("DeleteRequest")) {
   593	                    JsonNode key = writeRequest.get("DeleteRequest").get("Key");
   594	                    deleteItem(tableName, key, region);
   595	                }
   596	            }
   597	        }
   598	        return new BatchWriteResult(Map.of());
   599	    }
   600	
   601	    public record BatchGetResult(Map<String, List<JsonNode>> responses, Map<String, JsonNode> unprocessedKeys) {}
   602	
   603	    public BatchGetResult batchGetItem(Map<String, JsonNode> requestItems, String region) {
   604	        Map<String, List<JsonNode>> responses = new HashMap<>();
   605	        for (Map.Entry<String, JsonNode> entry : requestItems.entrySet()) {
   606	            String tableName = entry.getKey();
   607	            JsonNode tableRequest = entry.getValue();
   608	            JsonNode keys = tableRequest.get("Keys");
   609	            List<JsonNode> tableItems = new ArrayList<>();
   610	            if (keys != null && keys.isArray()) {
   611	                for (JsonNode key : keys) {
   612	                    JsonNode item = getItem(tableName, key, region);
   613	                    if (item != null) {
   614	                        tableItems.add(item);
   615	                    }
   616	                }
   617	            }
   618	            responses.put(tableName, tableItems);
   619	        }
   620	        return new BatchGetResult(responses, Map.of());

   458	        if (!streamSpec.isMissingNode()) {
   459	            boolean streamEnabled = streamSpec.path("StreamEnabled").asBoolean(false);
   460	            if (streamEnabled) {
   461	                String viewType = streamSpec.path("StreamViewType").asText("NEW_AND_OLD_IMAGES");
   462	                StreamDescription sd = dynamoDbStreamService.enableStream(
   463	                        tableName, table.getTableArn(), viewType, region);
   464	                table.setStreamEnabled(true);
   465	                table.setStreamArn(sd.getStreamArn());
   466	                table.setStreamViewType(viewType);
   467	            } else {
   468	                dynamoDbStreamService.disableStream(tableName, region);
   469	                table.setStreamEnabled(false);
   470	            }
   471	        }
   472	
   473	        ObjectNode response = objectMapper.createObjectNode();
   474	        response.set("TableDescription", tableToNode(table));
   475	        return Response.ok(response).build();
   476	    }
   477	
   478	    private Response handleDescribeTimeToLive(JsonNode request, String region) {
   479	        String tableName = request.path("TableName").asText();
   480	        TableDefinition table = dynamoDbService.describeTable(tableName, region);
   481	
   482	        ObjectNode response = objectMapper.createObjectNode();
   483	        ObjectNode ttlDesc = objectMapper.createObjectNode();
   484	        if (table.isTtlEnabled() && table.getTtlAttributeName() != null) {
   485	            ttlDesc.put("TimeToLiveStatus", "ENABLED");
   486	            ttlDesc.put("AttributeName", table.getTtlAttributeName());
   487	        } else {
   488	            ttlDesc.put("TimeToLiveStatus", "DISABLED");
   489	        }
   490	        response.set("TimeToLiveDescription", ttlDesc);

    21	@ApplicationScoped

    38	    public Response handle(String action, JsonNode request, String region) {
    39	        return switch (action) {
    40	            case "ListStreams" -> handleListStreams(request, region);
    41	            case "DescribeStream" -> handleDescribeStream(request, region);
    42	            case "GetShardIterator" -> handleGetShardIterator(request, region);
    43	            case "GetRecords" -> handleGetRecords(request, region);
    44	            default -> {
    45	                yield Response.status(400)
    46	                        .entity(new AwsErrorResponse("UnknownOperationException", "Operation " + action + " is not supported."))
    47	                        .build();
    48	            }
    49	        };
    50	    }
    51	
    52	    private Response handleListStreams(JsonNode request, String region) {
    53	        String tableNameFilter = request.has("TableName") ? request.get("TableName").asText() : null;
    54	
    55	        List<StreamDescription> streams = streamService.listStreams(tableNameFilter, region);
    56	
    57	        ObjectNode response = objectMapper.createObjectNode();
    58	        ArrayNode streamList = objectMapper.createArrayNode();
    59	        for (StreamDescription sd : streams) {
    60	            ObjectNode entry = objectMapper.createObjectNode();
    61	            entry.put("StreamArn", sd.getStreamArn());
    62	            entry.put("StreamLabel", sd.getStreamLabel());
    63	            entry.put("TableName", sd.getTableName());
    64	            streamList.add(entry);
    65	        }
    66	        response.set("Streams", streamList);
    67	        return Response.ok(response).build();
    68	    }
    69	
    70	    private Response handleDescribeStream(JsonNode request, String region) {
    71	        String streamArn = request.path("StreamArn").asText();
    72	        StreamDescription sd = streamService.describeStream(streamArn);
    73	
    74	        // Fetch key schema from the table
    75	        List<KeySchemaElement> keySchema = List.of();
    76	        try {
    77	            var table = dynamoDbService.describeTable(sd.getTableName(), region);
    78	            keySchema = table.getKeySchema();
    79	        } catch (Exception ignored) {
    80	        }
    81	
    82	        ObjectNode response = objectMapper.createObjectNode();
    83	        response.set("StreamDescription", describeStreamToNode(sd, keySchema));
    84	        return Response.ok(response).build();
    85	    }

    87	    private ObjectNode describeStreamToNode(StreamDescription sd, List<KeySchemaElement> keySchema) {
    88	        ObjectNode node = objectMapper.createObjectNode();
    89	        node.put("StreamArn", sd.getStreamArn());
    90	        node.put("StreamLabel", sd.getStreamLabel());
    91	        node.put("StreamStatus", sd.getStreamStatus());
    92	        node.put("StreamViewType", sd.getStreamViewType());
    93	        node.put("TableName", sd.getTableName());
    94	        node.put("CreationRequestDateTime", sd.getCreationDateTime().getEpochSecond());
    95	
    96	        ArrayNode keySchemaArray = objectMapper.createArrayNode();
    97	        for (KeySchemaElement ks : keySchema) {
    98	            ObjectNode ksNode = objectMapper.createObjectNode();
    99	            ksNode.put("AttributeName", ks.getAttributeName());
   100	            ksNode.put("KeyType", ks.getKeyType());
   101	            keySchemaArray.add(ksNode);
   102	        }
   103	        node.set("KeySchema", keySchemaArray);
   104	
   105	        ArrayNode shards = objectMapper.createArrayNode();
   106	        ObjectNode shard = objectMapper.createObjectNode();
   107	        shard.put("ShardId", DynamoDbStreamService.SHARD_ID);
   108	        ObjectNode seqRange = objectMapper.createObjectNode();
   109	        seqRange.put("StartingSequenceNumber", sd.getStartingSequenceNumber());
   110	        shard.set("SequenceNumberRange", seqRange);
   111	        shards.add(shard);
   112	        node.set("Shards", shards);
   113	
   114	        node.putNull("LastEvaluatedShardId");
   115	        return node;
   116	    }
   117	
   118	    private Response handleGetShardIterator(JsonNode request, String region) {
   119	        String streamArn = request.path("StreamArn").asText();
   120	        String shardId = request.path("ShardId").asText();
   121	        String iteratorType = request.path("ShardIteratorType").asText();
   122	        String sequenceNumber = request.has("SequenceNumber")
   123	                ? request.get("SequenceNumber").asText() : null;
   124	
   125	        String iterator = streamService.getShardIterator(streamArn, shardId, iteratorType, sequenceNumber);
   126	
   127	        ObjectNode response = objectMapper.createObjectNode();
   128	        response.put("ShardIterator", iterator);
   129	        return Response.ok(response).build();
   130	    }
   131	
   132	    private Response handleGetRecords(JsonNode request, String region) {
   133	        String shardIterator = request.path("ShardIterator").asText();
   134	        Integer limit = request.has("Limit") ? request.get("Limit").asInt() : null;
   135	
   136	        DynamoDbStreamService.GetRecordsResult result = streamService.getRecords(shardIterator, limit);
   137	
   138	        ObjectNode response = objectMapper.createObjectNode();
   139	        ArrayNode recordsArray = objectMapper.createArrayNode();
   140	        for (DynamoDbStreamRecord record : result.records()) {
   141	            recordsArray.add(recordToNode(record));
   142	        }
   143	        response.set("Records", recordsArray);
   144	        response.put("NextShardIterator", result.nextShardIterator());
   145	        
   146	        return Response.ok(response).build();
   147	    }
   148	
   149	    private ObjectNode recordToNode(DynamoDbStreamRecord record) {
   150	        ObjectNode node = objectMapper.createObjectNode();
   151	        node.put("eventID", record.getEventId());
   152	        node.put("eventName", record.getEventName());
   153	        node.put("eventVersion", record.getEventVersion());
   154	        node.put("eventSource", record.getEventSource());
   155	        node.put("awsRegion", record.getAwsRegion());
   156	
   157	        ObjectNode dynamodb = objectMapper.createObjectNode();
   158	        dynamodb.put("ApproximateCreationDateTime", record.getApproximateCreationDateTime());
   159	        if (record.getKeys() != null) {
   160	            dynamodb.set("Keys", record.getKeys());
   161	        }
   162	        if (record.getNewImage() != null) {
   163	            dynamodb.set("NewImage", record.getNewImage());
   164	        }
   165	        if (record.getOldImage() != null) {
   166	            dynamodb.set("OldImage", record.getOldImage());
   167	        }
   168	        dynamodb.put("SequenceNumber", record.getSequenceNumber());
   169	        dynamodb.put("SizeBytes", 100);
   170	        dynamodb.put("StreamViewType", record.getStreamViewType());
   171	        node.set("dynamodb", dynamodb);
   172	
   173	        return node;
   174	    }

     2	
     3	import io.github.hectorvent.floci.config.EmulatorConfig;
     4	import com.fasterxml.jackson.core.type.TypeReference;
     5	import jakarta.enterprise.context.ApplicationScoped;
     6	import jakarta.inject.Inject;
     7	import org.jboss.logging.Logger;
     8	
     9	import java.nio.file.Path;
    10	import java.util.ArrayList;
    11	import java.util.List;
    12	import java.util.Map;
    13	
    14	/**
    15	 * Factory that creates StorageBackend instances based on configuration.
    16	 * Tracks all created backends for lifecycle management.
    17	 */
    18	@ApplicationScoped
    19	public class StorageFactory {
    20	
    21	    private static final Logger LOG = Logger.getLogger(StorageFactory.class);
    22	
    23	    private final EmulatorConfig config;
    24	    private final List<StorageBackend<?, ?>> allBackends = new ArrayList<>();
    25	    private final List<HybridStorage<?, ?>> hybridBackends = new ArrayList<>();
    26	    private final List<WalStorage<?, ?>> walBackends = new ArrayList<>();
    27	
    28	    @Inject
    29	    public StorageFactory(EmulatorConfig config) {
    30	        this.config = config;
    31	    }
    32	
    33	    /**
    34	     * Create a storage backend for the given service.
    35	     *
    36	     * @param serviceName   the service name (ssm, sqs, s3)
    37	     * @param fileName      the JSON file name for persistent storage
    38	     * @param typeReference Jackson type reference for deserialization
    39	     */
    40	    public <K, V> StorageBackend<K, V> create(String serviceName, String fileName,
    41	                                               TypeReference<Map<K, V>> typeReference) {
    42	        String mode = resolveMode(serviceName);
    43	        long flushInterval = resolveFlushInterval(serviceName);
    44	        Path basePath = Path.of(config.storage().persistentPath());
    45	        Path filePath = basePath.resolve(fileName);
    46	
    47	        LOG.infov("Creating {0} storage for service {1} (file: {2})", mode, serviceName, filePath);
    48	
    49	        StorageBackend<K, V> backend = switch (mode) {
    50	            case "memory" -> new InMemoryStorage<>();
    51	            case "persistent" -> new PersistentStorage<>(filePath, typeReference);
    52	            case "hybrid" -> {
    53	                var hybrid = new HybridStorage<>(filePath, typeReference, flushInterval);
    54	                hybridBackends.add(hybrid);
    55	                yield hybrid;
    56	            }
    57	            case "wal" -> {
    58	                Path snapshotPath = basePath.resolve(fileName.replace(".json", "-snapshot.json"));
    59	                Path walFilePath = basePath.resolve(fileName.replace(".json", ".wal"));
    60	                long compactionInterval = config.storage().wal().compactionIntervalMs();
    61	                var wal = new WalStorage<>(snapshotPath, walFilePath, typeReference, compactionInterval);
    62	                walBackends.add(wal);
    63	                yield wal;
    64	            }
    65	            default -> throw new IllegalArgumentException("Unknown storage mode: " + mode);
    66	        };
    67	
    68	        // load because loadAll() may run before the service is initialized
    69	        backend.load();
    70	
    71	        allBackends.add(backend);
    72	        return backend;
    73	    }
    74	
    75	    /** Load all storage backends from disk. */
    76	    public void loadAll() {
    77	        for (StorageBackend<?, ?> backend : allBackends) {
    78	            backend.load();
    79	        }
    80	    }
    81	
    82	    /** Flush all storage backends to disk. */
    83	    public void flushAll() {
    84	        for (StorageBackend<?, ?> backend : allBackends) {
    85	            backend.flush();
    86	        }
    87	    }
    88	
    89	    /** Shutdown all managed backends (stop schedulers, close connections). */
    90	    public void shutdownAll() {
    91	        for (HybridStorage<?, ?> hybrid : hybridBackends) {
    92	            hybrid.shutdown();
    93	        }
    94	        for (WalStorage<?, ?> wal : walBackends) {
    95	            wal.shutdown();
    96	        }
    97	        flushAll();
    98	    }
    99	
   100	    private String resolveMode(String serviceName) {
   101	        String globalMode = config.storage().mode();
   102	        return switch (serviceName) {
   103	            case "ssm" -> config.storage().services().ssm().mode().orElse(globalMode);
   104	            case "sqs" -> config.storage().services().sqs().mode().orElse(globalMode);
   105	            case "s3" -> config.storage().services().s3().mode().orElse(globalMode);
   106	            case "dynamodb" -> config.storage().services().dynamodb().mode().orElse(globalMode);
   107	            case "sns" -> config.storage().services().sns().mode().orElse(globalMode);
   108	            case "lambda" -> config.storage().services().lambda().mode().orElse(globalMode);
   109	            case "cloudwatchlogs" -> config.storage().services().cloudwatchlogs().mode().orElse(globalMode);
   110	            case "cloudwatchmetrics" -> config.storage().services().cloudwatchmetrics().mode().orElse(globalMode);
   111	            case "secretsmanager" -> config.storage().services().secretsmanager().mode().orElse(globalMode);
   112	            case "opensearch" -> config.storage().services().opensearch().mode().orElse(globalMode);
   113	            default -> globalMode;
   114	        };
   115	    }
   116	
   117	    private long resolveFlushInterval(String serviceName) {
   118	        return switch (serviceName) {
   119	            case "ssm" -> config.storage().services().ssm().flushIntervalMs();
   120	            case "dynamodb" -> config.storage().services().dynamodb().flushIntervalMs();
   121	            case "sns" -> config.storage().services().sns().flushIntervalMs();
   122	            case "lambda" -> config.storage().services().lambda().flushIntervalMs();
   123	            case "cloudwatchlogs" -> config.storage().services().cloudwatchlogs().flushIntervalMs();
   124	            case "cloudwatchmetrics" -> config.storage().services().cloudwatchmetrics().flushIntervalMs();
   125	            case "secretsmanager" -> config.storage().services().secretsmanager().flushIntervalMs();
   126	            case "opensearch" -> config.storage().services().opensearch().flushIntervalMs();
   127	            default -> 5000L;
   128	        };
   129	    }
   130	}

     1	package io.github.hectorvent.floci.core.storage;
     2	
     3	import java.util.ArrayList;
     4	import java.util.Collections;
     5	import java.util.List;
     6	import java.util.Optional;
     7	import java.util.Set;
     8	import java.util.concurrent.ConcurrentHashMap;
     9	import java.util.function.Predicate;
    10	
    11	/**
    12	 * Thread-safe in-memory storage backed by ConcurrentHashMap.
    13	 * No persistence — data is lost on shutdown unless explicitly flushed.
    14	 */
    15	public class InMemoryStorage<K, V> implements StorageBackend<K, V> {
    16	
    17	    private final ConcurrentHashMap<K, V> store = new ConcurrentHashMap<>();
    18	
    19	    @Override
    20	    public void put(K key, V value) {
    21	        store.put(key, value);
    22	    }
    23	
    24	    @Override
    25	    public Optional<V> get(K key) {
    26	        return Optional.ofNullable(store.get(key));
    27	    }
    28	
    29	    @Override
    30	    public void delete(K key) {
    31	        store.remove(key);
    32	    }
    33	
    34	    @Override
    35	    public List<V> scan(Predicate<K> keyFilter) {
    36	        List<V> result = new ArrayList<>();
    37	        store.forEach((k, v) -> {
    38	            if (keyFilter.test(k)) {
    39	                result.add(v);
    40	            }
    41	        });
    42	        return result;
    43	    }
    44	
    45	    @Override
    46	    public Set<K> keys() {
    47	        return Collections.unmodifiableSet(store.keySet());
    48	    }
    49	
    50	    @Override
    51	    public void flush() {
    52	        // No-op for in-memory storage
    53	    }
    54	
    55	    @Override
    56	    public void load() {
    57	        // No-op for in-memory storage
    58	    }
    59	
    60	    @Override
    61	    public void clear() {
    62	        store.clear();
    63	    }
    64	}

Here's the result of running `cat -n` on /testbed/src/main/java/io/github/hectorvent/floci/core/storage/PersistentStorage.java:
     1	package io.github.hectorvent.floci.core.storage;
     2	
     3	import com.fasterxml.jackson.core.type.TypeReference;
     4	import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.ObjectMapper;
     5	import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.SerializationFeature;
     6	import com.fasterxml.jackson.datatype.jsr310.JavaTimeModule;
     7	import org.jboss.logging.Logger;
     8	
     9	import java.io.IOException;
    10	import java.nio.file.Files;
    11	import java.nio.file.Path;
    12	import java.nio.file.StandardCopyOption;
    13	import java.util.Collections;
    14	import java.util.List;
    15	import java.util.Map;
    16	import java.util.Optional;
    17	import java.util.Set;
    18	import java.util.concurrent.ConcurrentHashMap;
    19	import java.util.function.Predicate;
    20	
    21	/**
    22	 * JSON file-backed persistent storage.
    23	 * Loads all data into memory on startup for fast reads.
    24	 * Write-through on every put/delete.
    25	 * Uses atomic writes (temp file + rename) for safety.
    26	 */
    27	public class PersistentStorage<K, V> implements StorageBackend<K, V> {
    28	
    29	    private static final Logger LOG = Logger.getLogger(PersistentStorage.class);
    30	
    31	    private final ConcurrentHashMap<K, V> store = new ConcurrentHashMap<>();
    32	    private final Path filePath;
    33	    private final ObjectMapper objectMapper;
    34	    private final TypeReference<Map<K, V>> typeReference;
    35	
    36	    public PersistentStorage(Path filePath, TypeReference<Map<K, V>> typeReference) {
    37	        this.filePath = filePath;
    38	        this.typeReference = typeReference;
    39	        this.objectMapper = new ObjectMapper();
    40	        this.objectMapper.registerModule(new JavaTimeModule());
    41	        this.objectMapper.disable(SerializationFeature.WRITE_DATES_AS_TIMESTAMPS);
    42	        this.objectMapper.enable(SerializationFeature.INDENT_OUTPUT);
    43	    }
    44	
    45	    @Override
    46	    public void put(K key, V value) {
    47	        store.put(key, value);
    48	        persistToDisk();
    49	    }
    50	
    51	    @Override
    52	    public Optional<V> get(K key) {
    53	        return Optional.ofNullable(store.get(key));
    54	    }
    55	
    56	    @Override
    57	    public void delete(K key) {
    58	        store.remove(key);
    59	        persistToDisk();
    60	    }
    61	
    62	    @Override
    63	    public List<V> scan(Predicate<K> keyFilter) {
    64	        return store.entrySet().stream()
    65	                .filter(e -> keyFilter.test(e.getKey()))
    66	                .map(Map.Entry::getValue)
    67	                .toList();
    68	    }
    69	
    70	    @Override
    71	    public Set<K> keys() {
    72	        return Collections.unmodifiableSet(store.keySet());
    73	    }
    74	
    75	    @Override
    76	    public void flush() {
    77	        persistToDisk();
    78	    }
    79	
    80	    @Override
    81	    public void load() {
    82	        if (!Files.exists(filePath)) {
    83	            LOG.debugv("No persistent file found at {0}, starting with empty store", filePath);
    84	            return;
    85	        }
    86	        try {
    87	            Map<K, V> data = objectMapper.readValue(filePath.toFile(), typeReference);
    88	            store.clear();
    89	            store.putAll(data);
    90	            LOG.infov("Loaded {0} entries from {1}", store.size(), filePath);
    91	        } catch (IOException e) {
    92	            LOG.errorv(e, "Failed to load data from {0}", filePath);
    93	        }
    94	    }
    95	
    96	    @Override
    97	    public void clear() {
    98	        store.clear();
    99	        persistToDisk();
   100	    }
   101	
   102	    private synchronized void persistToDisk() {
   103	        try {
   104	            Files.createDirectories(filePath.getParent());
   105	            Path tempFile = filePath.resolveSibling(filePath.getFileName() + ".tmp");
   106	            objectMapper.writeValue(tempFile.toFile(), store);
   107	            Files.move(tempFile, filePath, StandardCopyOption.REPLACE_EXISTING, StandardCopyOption.ATOMIC_MOVE);
   108	        } catch (IOException e) {
   109	            LOG.errorv(e, "Failed to persist data to {0}", filePath);
   110	        }
   111	    }
   112	}
   113

import io.github.hectorvent.floci.core.common.RegionResolver;
import io.github.hectorvent.floci.core.storage.InMemoryStorage;
import io.github.hectorvent.floci.services.dynamodb.DynamoDbService;
import io.github.hectorvent.floci.services.dynamodb.DynamoDbStreamService;
import io.github.hectorvent.floci.services.dynamodb.model.*;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.ObjectMapper;
import java.util.*;

public class ReproDdbStreams {
  public static void main(String[] args) {
    var tableStore = new InMemoryStorage<String, TableDefinition>();
    String region = "us-east-1";
    var table = new TableDefinition("T", List.of(new KeySchemaElement("id", "HASH")),
        List.of(new AttributeDefinition("id", "S")), region, "000000000000");
    table.setStreamEnabled(true);
    table.setStreamArn(table.getTableArn() + "/stream/2025-01-01T00:00:00.000");
    table.setStreamViewType("NEW_AND_OLD_IMAGES");
    tableStore.put(region + "::T", table);

    var streamService = new DynamoDbStreamService(new ObjectMapper());
    new DynamoDbService(tableStore, null, new RegionResolver(region, "000000000000"), streamService);

    var streams = streamService.listStreams(null, region);
    System.out.println("streams=" + streams.size());
    if (streams.isEmpty()) {
      System.exit(1);
    }
  }
}

   723	        return results;
   724	    }
   725	
   726	    // --- UpdateTable ---
   727	
   728	    public TableDefinition updateTable(String tableName, Long readCapacity, Long writeCapacity, String region) {
   729	        return updateTable(tableName, readCapacity, writeCapacity, List.of(), List.of(), List.of(), region);
   730	    }
   731	
   732	    public TableDefinition updateTable(String tableName, Long readCapacity, Long writeCapacity,
   733	                                        List<GlobalSecondaryIndex> gsiCreates, List<String> gsiDeletes,
   734	                                        List<AttributeDefinition> newAttrDefs, String region) {
   735	        String storageKey = regionKey(region, tableName);
   736	        TableDefinition table = tableStore.get(storageKey)
   737	                .orElseThrow(() -> resourceNotFoundException(tableName));
   738	
   739	        if (readCapacity != null) {
   740	            table.getProvisionedThroughput().setReadCapacityUnits(readCapacity);
   741	        }
   742	        if (writeCapacity != null) {
   743	            table.getProvisionedThroughput().setWriteCapacityUnits(writeCapacity);
   744	        }
   745	
   746	        for (String indexName : gsiDeletes) {
   747	            table.getGlobalSecondaryIndexes().removeIf(g -> indexName.equals(g.getIndexName()));
   748	        }
   749	
   750	        for (GlobalSecondaryIndex gsi : gsiCreates) {
   751	            gsi.setIndexArn(table.getTableArn() + "/index/" + gsi.getIndexName());
   752	            table.getGlobalSecondaryIndexes().add(gsi);
   753	        }
   754	
   755	        if (newAttrDefs != null && !newAttrDefs.isEmpty()) {
   756	            List<AttributeDefinition> existing = table.getAttributeDefinitions();
   757	            for (AttributeDefinition newDef : newAttrDefs) {
   758	                boolean found = existing.stream()
   759	                        .anyMatch(e -> e.getAttributeName().equals(newDef.getAttributeName()));
   760	                if (!found) {
   761	                    existing.add(newDef);
   762	                }
   763	            }
   764	        }
   765	
   766	        tableStore.put(storageKey, table);
   767	        LOG.infov("Updated table: {0} in region {1}", tableName, region);
   768	        return table;
   769	    }
   770	
   771	    // --- TTL ---
   772	
   773	    public void updateTimeToLive(String tableName, String ttlAttributeName, boolean enabled, String region) {
   774	        String storageKey = regionKey(region, tableName);
   775	        TableDefinition table = tableStore.get(storageKey)
   776	                .orElseThrow(() -> resourceNotFoundException(tableName));
   777	        table.setTtlAttributeName(ttlAttributeName);
   778	        table.setTtlEnabled(enabled);
   779	        tableStore.put(storageKey, table);
   780	        LOG.infov("Updated TTL for table {0}: enabled={1}, attr={2}", tableName, enabled, ttlAttributeName);
   781	    }
   782	
   783	    static boolean isExpired(JsonNode item, TableDefinition table) {
   784	        if (!table.isTtlEnabled() || table.getTtlAttributeName() == null) return false;
   785	        JsonNode attr = item.get(table.getTtlAttributeName());
   786	        if (attr == null || !attr.has("N")) return false;
   787	        try {
   788	            return Long.parseLong(attr.get("N").asText()) < Instant.now().getEpochSecond();
   789	        } catch (NumberFormatException e) {
   790	            return false;
   791	        }
   792	    }
   793	
   794	    void deleteExpiredItems() {
   795	        int totalDeleted = 0;
   796	        for (String storageKey : tableStore.keys()) {
   797	            TableDefinition table = tableStore.get(storageKey).orElse(null);
   798	            if (table == null || !table.isTtlEnabled() || table.getTtlAttributeName() == null) {
   799	                continue;
   800	            }
   801	            var items = itemsByTable.get(storageKey);
   802	            if (items == null) continue;
   803	
   804	            List<String> expiredKeys = items.entrySet().stream()
   805	                    .filter(e -> isExpired(e.getValue(), table))
   806	                    .map(Map.Entry::getKey)
   807	                    .toList();
   808	
   809	            if (expiredKeys.isEmpty()) continue;
   810	
   811	            String region = storageKey.split("::", 2)[0];
   812	            for (String itemKey : expiredKeys) {
   813	                JsonNode removed = items.remove(itemKey);
   814	                if (removed != null && streamService != null) {
   815	                    streamService.captureEvent(table.getTableName(), "REMOVE", removed, null, table, region);
   816	                }
   817	            }
   818	            persistItems(storageKey);
   819	            totalDeleted += expiredKeys.size();
   820	        }
   821	        if (totalDeleted > 0) {
   822	            LOG.infov("TTL sweeper removed {0} expired items", totalDeleted);
   823	        }
   824	    }
   825	
   826	    // --- Tag Operations ---
   827	
   828	    public void tagResource(String resourceArn, Map<String, String> tags, String region) {
   829	        TableDefinition table = findTableByArn(resourceArn, region);
   830	        if (table.getTags() == null) {
   831	            table.setTags(new HashMap<>());
   832	        }
   833	        table.getTags().putAll(tags);
   834	        String storageKey = regionKey(region, table.getTableName());
   835	        tableStore.put(storageKey, table);
   836	        LOG.debugv("Tagged resource: {0}", resourceArn);
   837	    }
   838	
   839	    public void untagResource(String resourceArn, List<String> tagKeys, String region) {
   840	        TableDefinition table = findTableByArn(resourceArn, region);
   841	        if (table.getTags() != null) {
   842	            for (String key : tagKeys) {
   843	                table.getTags().remove(key);
   844	            }
   845	            String storageKey = regionKey(region, table.getTableName());
   846	            tableStore.put(storageKey, table);
   847	        }
   848	        LOG.debugv("Untagged resource: {0}", resourceArn);
   849	    }
   850	
   851	    public Map<String, String> listTagsOfResource(String resourceArn, String region) {
   852	        TableDefinition table = findTableByArn(resourceArn, region);
   853	        return table.getTags() != null ? table.getTags() : Map.of();
   854	    }
   855	
   856	    private TableDefinition findTableByArn(String arn, String region) {
   857	        String prefix = region + "::";
   858	        return tableStore.scan(k -> k.startsWith(prefix)).stream()
   859	                .filter(t -> arn.equals(t.getTableArn()))
   860	                .findFirst()
   861	                .orElseThrow(() -> new AwsException("ResourceNotFoundException",
   862	                        "Requested resource not found: " + arn, 400));
   863	    }
   864

   868	                                    JsonNode exprAttrNames, JsonNode exprAttrValues) {
   869	        if (!matchesFilterExpression(existingItem, conditionExpression, exprAttrNames, exprAttrValues)) {
   870	            throw new AwsException("ConditionalCheckFailedException",

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
cd /testbed
rm -rf /tmp/repro-ddb && mkdir -p /tmp/repro-ddb/io/github/hectorvent/floci/services/dynamodb /tmp/repro-ddb/classes
cat > /tmp/repro-ddb/io/github/hectorvent/floci/services/dynamodb/ReproDdbStreams.java <<'JAVA'
package io.github.hectorvent.floci.services.dynamodb;

import io.github.hectorvent.floci.core.common.RegionResolver;
import io.github.hectorvent.floci.core.storage.InMemoryStorage;
import io.github.hectorvent.floci.services.dynamodb.model.*;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.ObjectMapper;
import java.util.*;

public class ReproDdbStreams {
  public static void main(String[] args) {
    var tableStore = new InMemoryStorage<String, TableDefinition>();
    String region = "us-east-1";
    var table = new TableDefinition("T", List.of(new KeySchemaElement("id", "HASH")),
        List.of(new AttributeDefinition("id", "S")), region, "000000000000");
    table.setStreamEnabled(true);
    table.setStreamArn(table.getTableArn() + "/stream/2025-01-01T00:00:00.000");
    table.setStreamViewType("NEW_AND_OLD_IMAGES");
    tableStore.put(region + "::T", table);

    var streamService = new DynamoDbStreamService(new ObjectMapper());
    new DynamoDbService(tableStore, null, new RegionResolver(region, "000000000000"), streamService);

    var streams = streamService.listStreams(null, region);
    System.out.println("streams=" + streams.size());
    if (streams.isEmpty()) {
      System.exit(1);
    }
  }
}
JAVA

package io.github.hectorvent.floci.services.dynamodb;

import io.github.hectorvent.floci.core.common.RegionResolver;
import io.github.hectorvent.floci.core.storage.InMemoryStorage;
import io.github.hectorvent.floci.services.dynamodb.model.*;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.ObjectMapper;
import java.util.*;

public class ReproDdbStreams {
  public static void main(String[] args) {
    var tableStore = new InMemoryStorage<String, TableDefinition>();
    String region = "us-east-1";
    var table = new TableDefinition("T", List.of(new KeySchemaElement("id", "HASH")),
        List.of(new AttributeDefinition("id", "S")), region, "000000000000");
    table.setStreamEnabled(true);
    table.setStreamArn(table.getTableArn() + "/stream/2025-01-01T00:00:00.000");
    table.setStreamViewType("NEW_AND_OLD_IMAGES");
    tableStore.put(region + "::T", table);

    var streamService = new DynamoDbStreamService(new ObjectMapper());
    new DynamoDbService(tableStore, null, new RegionResolver(region, "000000000000"), streamService);

    var streams = streamService.listStreams(null, region);
    System.out.println("streams=" + streams.size());
    if (streams.isEmpty()) {
      System.exit(1);
    }
  }
}
JAVA

    public void restoreStream(TableDefinition table, String region) {
        if (table == null || !table.isStreamEnabled() || table.getStreamArn() == null) {
            return;
        }

        String tableName = table.getTableName();
        String streamArn = table.getStreamArn();
        String key = streamKey(region, tableName);
        streams.computeIfAbsent(key, ignored -> {
            StreamDescription sd = new StreamDescription();
            sd.setStreamArn(streamArn);
            sd.setStreamLabel(extractStreamLabel(streamArn));
            sd.setStreamStatus("ENABLED");
            sd.setStreamViewType(table.getStreamViewType() != null
                    ? table.getStreamViewType() : "NEW_AND_OLD_IMAGES");
            sd.setTableName(tableName);
            sd.setCreationDateTime(parseStreamCreationTime(sd.getStreamLabel()));
            sd.setStartingSequenceNumber(String.format("%021d", 1));
            return sd;
        });
        records.computeIfAbsent(streamArn, ignored -> new ConcurrentLinkedDeque<>());
    }

    private String extractStreamLabel(String streamArn) {
        int idx = streamArn.lastIndexOf("/stream/");
        return idx >= 0 ? streamArn.substring(idx + "/stream/".length()) : null;
    }

    private Instant parseStreamCreationTime(String streamLabel) {
        if (streamLabel == null) {
            return Instant.now();
        }
        try {
            return LocalDateTime.parse(streamLabel, STREAM_LABEL_FORMAT).toInstant(ZoneOffset.UTC);
        } catch (DateTimeParseException e) {
            return Instant.now();
        }
    }

    51	    public StreamDescription enableStream(String tableName, String tableArn, String viewType, String region) {
    52	        String key = streamKey(region, tableName);
    53	        StreamDescription existing = streams.get(key);
    54	        if (existing != null && "ENABLED".equals(existing.getStreamStatus())) {
    55	            return existing;
    56	        }
    57	
    58	        Instant now = Instant.now();
    59	        String label = STREAM_LABEL_FORMAT.format(now);
    60	        String streamArn = tableArn + "/stream/" + label;
    61	
    62	        StreamDescription sd = new StreamDescription();
    63	        sd.setStreamArn(streamArn);
    64	        sd.setStreamLabel(label);
    65	        sd.setStreamStatus("ENABLED");
    66	        sd.setStreamViewType(viewType);
    67	        sd.setTableName(tableName);
    68	        sd.setCreationDateTime(now);
    69	        sd.setStartingSequenceNumber(String.format("%021d", 1));
    70	
    71	        streams.put(key, sd);
    72	        records.put(streamArn, new ConcurrentLinkedDeque<>());
    73	        LOG.infov("Enabled stream for table {0} in region {1}: {2}", tableName, region, streamArn);

   117	    public void disableStream(String tableName, String region) {
   118	        String key = streamKey(region, tableName);

+    public void restoreStream(TableDefinition table, String region) {
+        if (table == null || !table.isStreamEnabled() || table.getStreamArn() == null) {
+            return;
+        }
+
+        String tableName = table.getTableName();
+        String streamArn = table.getStreamArn();
+        String key = streamKey(region, tableName);
+        streams.computeIfAbsent(key, ignored -> {
+            StreamDescription sd = new StreamDescription();
+            sd.setStreamArn(streamArn);
+            sd.setStreamLabel(extractStreamLabel(streamArn));
+            sd.setStreamStatus("ENABLED");
+            sd.setStreamViewType(table.getStreamViewType() != null
+                    ? table.getStreamViewType() : "NEW_AND_OLD_IMAGES");
+            sd.setTableName(tableName);
+            sd.setCreationDateTime(parseStreamCreationTime(sd.getStreamLabel()));
+            sd.setStartingSequenceNumber(String.format("%021d", 1));
+            return sd;
+        });
+        records.computeIfAbsent(streamArn, ignored -> new ConcurrentLinkedDeque<>());
+    }
+
+    private String extractStreamLabel(String streamArn) {
+        int idx = streamArn.lastIndexOf("/stream/");
+        return idx >= 0 ? streamArn.substring(idx + "/stream/".length()) : null;
+    }
+
+    private Instant parseStreamCreationTime(String streamLabel) {
+        if (streamLabel == null) {
+            return Instant.now();
+        }
+        try {
+            return LocalDateTime.parse(streamLabel, STREAM_LABEL_FORMAT).toInstant(ZoneOffset.UTC);
+        } catch (DateTimeParseException e) {
+            return Instant.now();
+        }
+    }
+
     public void disableStream(String tableName, String region) {
         String key = streamKey(region, tableName);
         StreamDescription sd = streams.get(key);

</diff>
